country_event = { #intro 1
	id = austriaintro.1
	title = austriaintro.1.t
	desc = austriaintro.1.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_map_AH

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #k
		name = austriaintro.1.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = austriaintro.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
            limit = {
                is_ai = no
            }
            set_country_flag = PORTRAIT_PICKER_ACTIVE
        }
	}
}

country_event = { #Government paralyzed! (The constituents and Austria are bickering about what to do.)
	id = bdeausel.0
	title = bdeausel.0.t
	desc = bdeausel.0.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_empty_legislature

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #We need a new government! Attempt to hold a vote of no confidence!
		name = bdeausel.0.a
		AUS_add_three_collapse = yes
		ALL_add_five_collapse = yes
		add_political_power = -40
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausel.1
				days = 4
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}
	
}

country_event = { #Streeruwitz Government Resigns
	id = bdeausel.1
	title = bdeausel.1.t
	desc = bdeausel.1.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_streeruwitz_toast

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Auf Wiedersehen, Streeruwitz!
		name = bdeausel.1.a
		#Replace Streeruwitz with Ender
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				add_idea = AUS_Otto_Ender_hog_sco
				remove_idea = AUS_Ernst_Streeruwitz_hog_ade
			}
			end_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat}
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:paternal_autocrat}
			add_to_coalition = yes
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausel.24
				days = 4
				random = 48
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausel.2
				days = 20
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}
	
}

country_event = { #The CS in Disarray
	id = bdeausel.2
	title = bdeausel.2.t
	desc = bdeausel.2.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_declarations

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Appoint Miklas - we need experience!
		name = bdeausel.2.a
		add_political_power = 20
		set_country_flag = AUS_1936_miklas
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausel.15
				days = 7
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Appoint Ender - we need experience!
		name = bdeausel.2.b
		add_political_power = 20
		set_country_flag = AUS_1936_ender
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausel.15
				days = 7
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Appoint Dollfuss!
		name = bdeausel.2.c
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { AUS.VF_split > 0.99 }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausel.25
					days = 7
					random = 48
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #We can't risk anything - appoint Buresch!
		name = bdeausel.2.e
		add_stability = 0.03
		add_political_power = 10
		set_global_flag = AUS_BURESCH
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausel.26
				days = 5
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}
	
}

country_event = { #Kalergi Casts a Bid
	id = bdeausel.3
	title = bdeausel.3.t
	desc = {
        text = bdeausel.3.d.a #with Dolbuss
        trigger = {
			has_global_flag = AUS_VF_SPLIT
        }
    }
	desc = {
        text = bdeausel.3.d.b #no bussy
        trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = AUS_VF_SPLIT
			}
        }
    }
	
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_kalergi_speech

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Gather your votes...
		name = bdeausel.3.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.025
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Snap Election Announced!
	id = bdeausel.4
	title = bdeausel.4.t
	desc = bdeausel.4.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_legislature_protest

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Gather your votes...
		name = bdeausel.4.a
		add_stability = 0.01
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = AUS_VF_SPLIT
				}
				country_event = { #VF coalition
					id = bdeausel.5
					days = 6
					random = 48
				}
			}
			country_event = { #CS coalition
				id = bdeausel.6
				days = 4
				random = 48
			}
			country_event = { #DBP coalition
				id = bdeausel.7
				days = 9
				random = 48
			}
			
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausel.2
				days = 6
				random = 48
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausel.8
				days = 30
				random = 240
			}
		}
		
	}
}

country_event = { #Election
	id = bdeausel.8
	title = bdeausel.8.t
	desc = bdeausel.8.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_suffrage

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #The CS is elected
		name = bdeausel.8.a
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = 0.03
		remove_all_ministers_but_for = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = AUS_VF_SPLIT
			}
			set_country_flag = AUS_CS_WON
			
			complete_national_focus = AUS_cs_reign_continues
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = AUS_1936_miklas
				}
				set_country_flag = AUS_MINISTERPREZ_MIKLAS
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_conservative
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					popularity = 0.03
				}
				add_authdem_to_coalition = yes
				add_ideas = {
					AUS_Wilhelm_Miklas_hog_sco
					AUS_Julius_Raab_eco_sco
					AUS_Richard_Schmitz_sec_sco
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = AUS_1936_ender
				}
				set_country_flag = AUS_MINISTERPREZ_ENDER
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_conservative
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					popularity = 0.03
				}
				add_authdem_to_coalition = yes
				add_ideas = {
					AUS_Otto_Ender_hog_sco
					AUS_Eduard_Heinl_eco_sco
					AUS_Rudolf_Ramek_sec_sco
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = AUS_BURESCH
				}
				set_country_flag = AUS_MINISTERPREZ_BURESCH
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					popularity = 0.03
				}
				add_soccon_to_coalition = yes
				add_ideas = {
					AUS_Karl_Buresch_hog_ade
					AUS_Engelbert_Dollfuss_eco_ade
					AUS_Carl_Vaugoin_sec_ade
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 0.03
			}
			
			add_soccon_to_coalition = yes
			add_pataut_to_coalition = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = AUS_1936_miklas
				}
				#create_country_leader = {
				#	name = "Wilhelm Miklas"
				#	desc = "POLITICS_MIKLAS_DESC"
				#	picture = "gfx/leaders/AUS/AUS_Wilhelm_Miklas.png"
				#	expire = "1965.1.1"
				#	ideology = social_conservative_subtype
				#}
				set_country_flag = AUS_MINISTERPREZ_MIKLAS
				complete_national_focus = AUS_cs_reign_continues
				add_ideas = {
					AUS_Wilhelm_Miklas_hog_sco
					AUS_Julius_Raab_eco_sco
					AUS_Richard_Schmitz_sec_sco
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = AUS_BURESCH
				}
				#create_country_leader = {
				#	name = "Karl Buresch"
				#	desc = "POLITICS_BURESCH_DESC"
				#	picture = "gfx/leaders/AUS/AUS_Karl_Buresch.png"
				#	expire = "1965.1.1"
				#	ideology = autdem_christian_democracy_subtype
				#}
				complete_national_focus = AUS_cs_reign_continues
				set_country_flag = AUS_CS_WON
				set_country_flag = AUS_VF_WON
				add_ideas = {
					AUS_Karl_Buresch_hog_ade
					AUS_Engelbert_Dollfuss_eco_ade
					AUS_Carl_Vaugoin_sec_ade
				}
			}	
			else = {
				#create_country_leader = {
				#	name = "Engelbert Dollfuss"
				#	desc = "POLITICS_DOLLFUSS_DESC"
				#	picture = "gfx/leaders/AUS/AUS_Engelbert_Dollfuss.png"
				#	expire = "1965.1.1"
				#	ideology = autdem_christian_democracy_subtype
				#}
				complete_national_focus = AUS_vf_usurpation
				set_country_flag = AUS_VF_WON
				set_country_flag = AUS_MINISTERPREZ_DOLLFUSS
				set_country_flag = AUS_AUTHDEM_DOLLFUSS
				add_ideas = {
					AUS_Engelbert_Dollfuss_hog_ade
					AUS_Julius_Raab_eco_sco
					AUS_Carl_Vaugoin_sec_ade
				}
			}
		}
		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = AUS_snap_election_complete
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausel.12
				days = 7
				random = 200
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Dollfuss is elected
		name = bdeausel.8.b
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = AUS_VF_SPLIT
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = 0.03
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
				var = AUS.revolution_value
				value = 2
			}
			set_country_flag = AUS_VF_WON
			set_country_flag = AUS_snap_election_complete
			complete_national_focus = AUS_vf_usurpation
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausel.9
				days = 7
				random = 200
			}

					has_completed_focus = DNB_to_save_the_empire
				}
			}

			}
		}
		if = {

				}
			}
			AUS_subtract_ten_collapse = yes
		}
	}

			}

				has_country_flag = AUS_bauer_1940
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = radical_socialist
			}
			add_socdem_to_coalition = yes

		}
	}
	
	option = { #DBP Victory

		}

		}

		}

country_event = { #Industrial building
	id = bdeaus.8
	title = bdeaus.8.t
	desc = bdeaus.8.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_karl_leaving_hungary

		
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = bdeaus.8.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = AUS_factory_flag_done
				}
			}
			THIS = {
				random_owned_state = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				}			
			}
			THIS_subtract_eight_collapse = yes
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = global.industrial_stuff
				value = 1
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = THIS.industrial_stuff_local
				value = 1
			}
			AUS = {
				scoped_sound_effect = "AUS_industrial_projects"
			}
			scoped_sound_effect = "AUS_industrial_projects"
			country_event = {
				id = bdeaus.8
				days = 40
			}
			set_country_flag = AUS_factory_flag_done
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = AUS_factory_flag
				clr_country_flag = AUS_factory_flag_done
			}
		}
	}
	
}

country_event = { #Austria Proposes Alliance - Add to faction
	id = bdeausfor.2
	title = bdeausfor.2.t
	desc = bdeausfor.2.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_BAN_big_speech2

	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #This will benefit us.
		name = bdeausfor.2.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }
		FROM = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = { AUS_DWV_member = yes }
					}
					country_event = {
						id = bdeausint.20
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						tag = BRA
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					country_event = {
						id = bdeausfor.106
						days = 3
						random = 72
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #We have no need for this.
		name = bdeausfor.2.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausfor.3
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Only if Venice is returned.
		name = bdeausfor.2.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = ITA
				tag = SRI
			}
			OR = {
				AUS = {
					owns_state = 160
					owns_state = 759
				}
				VNC = {
					is_subject_of = AUS
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausfor.20
				days = 5
				random = 24
			}
		}
	}
	
}

country_event = { #Austria Proposes Alliance (Imperial faction merge)
	id = bdeausfor.5
	title = bdeausfor.5.t
	desc = bdeausfor.5.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_BAN_big_speech2

	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #This will benefit us.
		name = bdeausfor.5.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			set_country_flag = AUS_faction_switch
		}
		ROOT = {
			add_to_faction = FROM
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = AUS_faction_switch
				}
				clr_country_flag = AUS_faction_switch
				PREV = {
					add_to_faction = PREV
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = AUS_alliance_partner
		}
	}
	
	option = { #We have no need for this.
		name = bdeausfor.5.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausfor.6
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
}

country_event = { #Transleithania Cuts Communications
	id = bdeausfor.11
	title = bdeausfor.11.t
	desc = bdeausfor.11.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_BAN_big_speech2

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #A distressing recall to 1848.
		name = bdeausfor.11.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		add_stability = -0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			HUN = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausfor.10
					days = 10
					random = 200
				}
				overlord = {
					end_puppet = ROOT
				}
				leave_faction = yes
				set_country_flag = AUS_CONST_about_to_revolt
			}
			FIU = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausfor.16
					days = 2
					random = 24
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit= {
					CZE = {
						OR = {
							has_government = authoritarian_democrat
							AND = {
								has_government = social_liberal
								AUS = {
									NOT = {
										has_government = social_liberal
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				CZE = {
					country_event = {
						id = bdeausfor.13
						days = 10
						random = 30
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Promise them the retention of full Hungarian autonomy.
		name = bdeausfor.11.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 200 }
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
			
		}
		HUN_add_ten_collapse = yes
		AUS_add_five_collapse = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit= {
					CZE = {
						OR = {
							has_government = authoritarian_democrat
							has_government = social_liberal
						}
					}
				}
				CZE = {
					country_event = {
						id = bdeausfor.13
						days = 10
						random = 30
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					GAL = {
						is_in_faction_with = AUS
					}
				}
				GAL = {
					country_event = {
						id = bdeausfor.12
						days = 15
						random = 150
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					CRO = {
						is_in_faction_with = AUS
					}
				}
				CRO = {
					country_event = {
						id = bdeausfor.12
						days = 15
						random = 150
					}
				}
			}
			HUN = {
				set_country_flag = AUS_promised_autonomy
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausfor.10
					days = 10
					random = 200
				}
			}
			FIU = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausfor.16
					days = 2
					random = 24
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			OR = {

			}
		}
	}
	
}

country_event = { #AUS - Bohemia Denies Absoluist Decree
	id = bdeausfor.14
	title = bdeausfor.14.t
	desc = bdeausfor.14.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_BAN_big_speech2

	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		CZE = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = AUS
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #All for the greater good, right?!
		name = bdeausfor.14.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		AUS_add_three_collapse = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_war_with = CZE
					has_war_with = HUN
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = AUS_absolutist_crisis_military_ticker
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = AUS_absolutist_crisis_military_ticker
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausdom.4 #Military Takeover event
				days = 20
				random = 100
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					GAL = {
						is_in_faction_with = AUS
					}
				}
				GAL = {
					country_event = {
						id = bdeausfor.12
						days = 15
						random = 150
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					CRO = {
						is_in_faction_with = AUS
					}
				}

				}

		}

			}
		}

		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Dealbreaker.
		name = bdeausfor.20.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		add_political_power = 20
		add_war_support = 0.05
	}
	
	option = { #Acceptable.
		name = bdeausfor.20.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		if = {
			limit = {

					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}

				ITA = {
					puppet = PREV
				}
				restore_previous_government_type = yes

		AUS = {

		}

			has_global_flag = AUS_UKR_war_refuses_surrender
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #It was worth a shot.
		name = bdeausfor.58.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					UKR = {
						surrender_progress > 0.5
					}
					AUS = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								controls_state = 198
								controls_state = 201
							}
							any_allied_country = {
								controls_state = 198
								controls_state = 201
							}
						}
						has_war_with = UKR
					}
				}
			}
			UKR = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausfor.59
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausfor.58
					days = 7
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = AUS.AUS_UKR_WAR_ticks
					value = 1
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						UKR = {
							OR = {
								controls_state = 1137
								controls_state = 1126
								controls_state = 1124
								controls_state = 43
								controls_state = 1129
								controls_state = 109
							}
						}
					}
					AUS = {
						country_event = {
							id = bdeausfor.63
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { AUS.AUS_UKR_WAR_ticks > 8 }
							check_variable = { AUS.AUS_UKR_WAR_ticks = 8 }
						}
					}
					country_event = {
						id = bdeausfor.61
					}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = global.extra_value_war_exhaust
						value = 0.007
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
	}
}

					has_country_flag = refused_surrender
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = global.extra_value_war_exhaust
				value = 0.002
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = THIS.austriaextra_value_war_exhaust
				value = 0.002
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = THIS.austriaextra_value_war_exhaust
				max = 0.015
				min = 0
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = global.extra_value_war_exhaust
				max = 0.015
				min = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = AUS_war_taking_too_long_event }
				}
				AUS = {
					country_event =  bdeausfor.78
					activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = AUS_peace_out }
					set_country_flag = AUS_war_taking_too_long_event
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Generic - Austria Sues for Peace with the Disadvantage
	id = bdeausfor.80
	title = bdeausfor.80.t
	desc = bdeausfor.80.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_BAN_big_speech2

		
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Acceptable terms
		name = bdeausfor.80.a
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.AUS_all_possible_array
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = AUS
						is_subject_of = AUS
					}
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
					owner = {
						set_country_flag = disadvantaged_loser
					}
					add_to_temp_array = { global.temp_states_austria_disadvantaged = THIS }
					owner = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									is_in_array = { global.temp_owners_austria_disadvantaged = THIS }
								}
							}
							add_to_temp_array = { global.temp_owners_austria_disadvantaged = THIS }
						}
					}
					ROOT = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			
		}
		
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.temp_owners_austria_disadvantaged
			save_event_target_as = disadvantaged_loser_target
			ROOT = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { global.temp_states_austria_disadvantaged = THIS }
						OR = {
							is_core_of = event_target:disadvantaged_loser_target
							is_claimed_by = event_target:disadvantaged_loser_target
						}
						NOT = {
							is_in_home_area = yes
						}
					}
					event_target:disadvantaged_loser_target = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		
		white_peace = AUS
	}
	
	option = { #We want to fight on
		name = bdeausfor.80.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		add_political_power = -75
		AUS = {
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = global.extra_value_war_exhaust
				value = THIS.austriaextra_value_war_exhaust
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = UKR
			}
			set_global_flag = AUS_UKR_war_refuses_surrender
			else = {
				set_country_flag = refused_surrender
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Fifth Balkan War - Hidden event that does stuffs
	id = bdeausfor.102
	title = bdeausfor.102.t
	desc = bdeausfor.102.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_karl_troops

		
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Gott erhalte Karl den Kaiser...
		name = bdeausfor.102.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = balkan_war_ended
				AUS = {
					has_war_with = SER
				}
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = fifth_balkan_war_ended
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SER = {
						has_capitulated = yes
					}
				}
				AUS = {
					country_event = bdeausfor.97
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROM = {
						has_capitulated = yes
					}
				}
				AUS = {
					country_event = bdeausfor.98
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SER = {
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = SKS
							tag = BOS
							tag = MNT
						}
						has_country_flag = BOTDE_ready_held_revolt
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt_owner
							has_global_flag = BPTROLL_revolt_incoming
							has_country_flag = BOTDE_AI_cheaty_method
						}
						exists = no
					}
					THIS = {
						set_country_flag = BPTROLL_revolt_start
						set_country_flag = BOTDE_AI_cheaty_method
						save_global_event_target_as = BOTDE_backer_revolt_tag
					}
					set_global_flag = BPTROLL_revolt_incoming
					set_global_flag = no_4_months
					SER = {
						scoped_sound_effect = "BOTDE_incoming_backer_revolt"
						activate_mission = SER_revolt_mission
					}
					AUS = {
						scoped_sound_effect = "BOTDE_incoming_backer_revolt"
						activate_mission = AUS_SER_revolt_mission
					}
					CRO = {
						scoped_sound_effect = "BOTDE_incoming_backer_revolt"
						activate_mission = AUS_SER_revolt_mission
					}
					SKS = {
						THIS_add_ten_collapse = yes
						set_variable_to_random = {
							var = THIS.extra_divs
							max = 3
							integer = yes
						}
					}
					BOS = {
						THIS_add_ten_collapse = yes
						set_variable_to_random = {
							var = THIS.extra_divs
							max = 3
							integer = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROM = {
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = SKS
							tag = BOS
							tag = MNT
						}
						has_country_flag = BOTDE_ready_held_revolt
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = BOTDE_imminent_minority_revolt_owner
							has_global_flag = BPTROLL_revolt_incoming
							has_country_flag = BOTDE_AI_cheaty_method
						}
						exists = no
					}
					
					THIS = {
						set_country_flag = BPTROLL_revolt_start
						set_country_flag = BOTDE_AI_cheaty_method
						save_global_event_target_as = BOTDE_backer_revolt_tag
					}
					set_global_flag = BPTROLL_revolt_incoming
					set_global_flag = no_4_months
					ROM = {
						scoped_sound_effect = "BOTDE_incoming_backer_revolt"
						activate_mission = ROM_revolt_mission
					}
					AUS = {
						scoped_sound_effect = "BOTDE_incoming_backer_revolt"
						activate_mission = AUS_ROM_revolt_mission
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							THIS = {
								tag = BUK
							}
						}
						GAL = {
							scoped_sound_effect = "BOTDE_incoming_backer_revolt"
							activate_mission = AUS_ROM_revolt_mission
						}
						else = {
							HUN = {
								scoped_sound_effect = "BOTDE_incoming_backer_revolt"
								activate_mission = AUS_ROM_revolt_mission
							}
						}
					}
					TRS = {
						THIS_add_ten_collapse = yes
						set_variable_to_random = {
							var = THIS.extra_divs
							max = 3
							integer = yes
						}
					}
					BAN = {
						THIS_add_ten_collapse = yes
						set_variable_to_random = {
							var = THIS.extra_divs
							max = 3
							integer = yes
						}
					}
					BUK = {
						THIS_add_ten_collapse = yes
						set_variable_to_random = {
							var = THIS.extra_divs
							max = 3
							integer = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		
			
			
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausfor.102
				days = 5
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = global.holyfuckimcumminglois
				value = 1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.holyfuckimcumminglois = 120 }
				}
				SER = {
					country_event = {
						id = bdeausfor.100
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Tyrolean Secession (scripted)
	id = bdeausfor.127
	title = bdeausfor.127.t
	desc = bdeausfor.127.d
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_tirol_poster

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Attack
		name = bdeausfor.127.a
		add_stability = -0.1
		ai_chance = { factor = 200 }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 153
					state = 39
					state = 942
					state = 783
				}
			}
			TYR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = AUS_tyrol_revolt
		
		TYR = {
			transfer_technology_without_doctrines = yes
			add_ideas = AUS_fighting_for_the_people
		}
		
		declare_war_on = {
			target = TYR
			type = annex_everything
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			TYR = {
				#country_event = const_oob.1 #Spawns divisions for TYR tag, hidden event
				REV_spawn_units = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = AWR
				}
				TYR = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = AWR
						type = annex_everything
					}
					
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausfor.128 #Heimwehr Militias Mobilize
				days = 3
				random = 72
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { TYR.collapse_appearance_value > 4 }
						check_variable = { TYR.collapse_appearance_value = 4 }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausfor.129 #Paramilitaries Join Forces
					days = 3
					random = 72
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_owned_state = {
						is_core_of = PGU
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausfor.146 #German-Bohemia Revolts
					days = 3
					random = 72
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Play as Tyrol
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		name = bdeausfor.127.b
		add_stability = -0.1
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 153
					state = 39
					state = 942
					state = 783
				}
			}
			TYR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = AUS_tyrol_revolt
		
		TYR = {
			transfer_technology_without_doctrines = yes
			add_ideas = AUS_fighting_for_the_people
		}
		
		declare_war_on = {
			target = TYR
			type = annex_everything
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			TYR = {
				#country_event = const_oob.1 #Spawns divisions for TYR tag, hidden event
				REV_spawn_units = yes
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausfor.128 #Heimwehr Militias Mobilize
				days = 3
				random = 72
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { TYR.collapse_appearance_value > 4 }
						check_variable = { TYR.collapse_appearance_value = 4 }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausfor.129 #Paramilitaries Join Forces
					days = 3
					random = 72
				}
			}
			TYR = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
		}
	}
}

				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = TYR
					}
					create_unit = { 
						division = "name = \"Territoriale brigade\" division_template = \"Territoriale brigade\" start_experience_factor = 1" 
						owner = PREV

					}
				}
				random_list = {
					70 = {

							division = "name = \"Territoriale brigade\" division_template = \"Territoriale brigade\" start_experience_factor = 1" 
							owner = PREV

					}
					30 = {
						create_unit = { 
							division = "name = \"Infanteriedivision mit Pionierbataillon\" division_template = \"Infanteriedivision mit Pionierbataillon\" start_experience_factor = 0.75" 
							owner = PREV
							allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					}

							is_claimed_by = PREV
						}

				}
				FROM = {
					remove_core_of = ROOT
					add_claim_by = ROOT
					clr_state_flag = BOTDE_defender_state_flag
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Plan for the Ausgleich
	id = bdeausgleich.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdeausgleich.1 ausgleich success: [?global.ausgleich_successes]" }
	title = bdeausgleich.1.t
	desc = bdeausgleich.1.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_legislature

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #No way. This is between us and the Magyars.
		name = bdeausgleich.1.a
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = HUN
		}
		HUN = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausgleich.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_conservative
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = global.ausgleich_successes
				value = 2
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = global.ausgleich_successes
					value = -1
				}
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = AUS_approaching_ausgleich
		set_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_hungary
		HUN_subtract_five_collapse = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausgleich.3
				days = 14
				random = 72
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Discuss this with just the 5 constituents.
		name = bdeausgleich.1.b
		add_political_power = -20
		AUS_fed_speed_2_add = yes
		HUN = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausgleich.5
				days = 1
			}
		}
		CRO = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausgleich.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
		CZE = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausgleich.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
		GAL = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausgleich.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = global.ausgleich_successes
				value = 1
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = AUS_approaching_ausgleich
		set_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_kingdoms
		ALL_subtract_five_collapse = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausgleich.3
				days = 14
				random = 72
			}
			HUN_add_five_collapse = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { #All peoples of the Empire must be able to participate.
		name = bdeausgleich.1.c
		add_political_power = -50
		AUS_fed_speed_2_add = yes
		HUN = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausgleich.5
				days = 1
			}
		}
		CRO = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausgleich.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
		CZE = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausgleich.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
		GAL = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausgleich.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = AUS_approaching_ausgleich
		set_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_peoples
		AUS_subtract_one_collapse = yes
		AUS_lower_all_minorities = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_government = radical_socialist
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = global.ausgleich_successes
				value = 2
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = global.ausgleich_successes
					value = -1
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausgleich.3
				days = 8
				random = 72
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausgleichflavor.4
				days = 15
				random = 72
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausgleichflavor.5
				days = 30
				random = 72
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Things are simply too dire. Postpone the Ausgleich.
		name = bdeausgleich.1.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { AUS.subject_revolt_progress > 0.8 }
				check_variable = { AUS.subject_revolt_progress = 0.8 }
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		add_political_power = -300
		#Start scripted collapse chain
	}
}

country_event = { #HUN - Austria extends ausgleich.
	id = bdeausgleich.5
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdeausgleich.5 ausgleich success: [?global.ausgleich_successes]" }
	title = {
		text = bdeausgleich.5.t_kingdoms
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_kingdoms
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = bdeausgleich.5.t_peoples
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_peoples
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = bdeausgleich.5.d_kingdoms
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_kingdoms
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = bdeausgleich.5.d_peoples
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_peoples
		}
	}
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_BAN_big_speech2

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { #Protest this slight.
		name = bdeausgleich.5.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					AUS = {
						is_ai = no
						check_variable = { AUS.subject_revolt_progress < 0.8 }
					}
					check_variable = { HUN.subject_revolt_progress < 0.05 }
					has_country_flag = HUN_always_accept_ausgleich_demands
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AUS
			modifier = BOTDE_AUS_hun_protested_ausgleich
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.ausgleich_successes
			value = -1
		}
		HUN_add_two_collapse = yes
		set_global_flag = HUN_protested_ausgleich
	}
	
	option = { #Boycott the Ausgleich.
		name = bdeausgleich.5.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { HUN.subject_revolt_progress > 0.8 }
				check_variable = { HUN.subject_revolt_progress = 0.8 }
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_always_accept_ausgleich_demands }
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.ausgleich_successes
			value = -2
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AUS
			modifier = BOTDE_AUS_hun_boycotted_ausgleich
		}
		HUN_add_five_collapse = yes
		set_global_flag = HUN_boycotted_ausgleich
		clr_country_flag = going_to_le_ausgleich
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { global.ausgleich_attendants = THIS.id }
			}
			remove_from_array = { global.ausgleich_attendants = THIS.id }
		}
	}
	
	option = { #It would only be self-sabotage.
		name = bdeausgleich.5.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					AUS = {
						is_ai = no
						check_variable = { AUS.subject_revolt_progress < 0.8 }
					}
					check_variable = { HUN.subject_revolt_progress < 0.05 }
					has_country_flag = HUN_always_accept_ausgleich_demands
				}
				add = 90
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AUS
			modifier = BOTDE_AUS_hun_attended_ausgleich
		}
		add_political_power = 10
		set_global_flag = HUN_no_protest
		set_country_flag = going_to_le_ausgleich
	}
}

			add_to_variable = {
				var = global.ausgleich_successes
				value = 1
			}
			add_political_power = -15
			add_stability = -0.03
			HUN_add_five_collapse = yes
			set_variable = { AUS.ausgleich_hungary_status_var = 3 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { HUN = { has_country_flag = HUN_ausgleich_ludicrous_fed_speed } }
			add_to_variable = {
				var = global.ausgleich_successes
				value = 1
			}
			add_political_power = -20
			add_stability = -0.05
			HUN = { 
				set_temp_variable = { revolt_progress_change = 0.075 }
				BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
			}
			set_variable = { AUS.ausgleich_hungary_status_var = 4 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = bdeausgleich.76.c
		trigger = {
			HUN = { HUN_ausgleich_pissed_off_over_fed_speed_trigger = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = -0.15
		ALL_add_ten_collapse = yes
		set_variable = { global.ausgleich_successes = -1 }
		HUN = {
			set_temp_variable = { revolt_progress_change = 0.20 }
			BOTDE_add_collapse = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausgleich.19
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Slovakia
	id = bdeausgleich.78
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdeausgleich.77 ausgleich success: [?global.ausgleich_successes]" }
	title = bdeausgleich.78.t
	desc = bdeausgleich.78.desc
	
	picture = GFX_event_HUN_poster

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	after = {
		country_event = {
			id = bdeausgleich.79
			days = 1
		}
	}

	option = { #Hungary
		name = bdeausgleich.78.a
		set_variable = { AUS.ausgleich_hungarian_revolt_slovakia_status_var = 1 }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SVK
			}
			transfer_state_to = HUN
		}
	}
	option = { #Bohemia
		name = bdeausgleich.78.b
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = CZE
		}
		set_variable = { AUS.ausgleich_hungarian_revolt_slovakia_status_var = 2 }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SVK
			}
			transfer_state_to = CZE
			add_core_of = CZE
		}
		CZE_subtract_ten_collapse = yes
	}
	option = { #Autonomy, Hungary puppet
		name = bdeausgleich.78.c
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = AUS_release_SVK_HUN
			set_variable = { AUS.ausgleich_hungarian_revolt_slovakia_status_var = 3 }
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = SVK
				}
				transfer_state_to = SVK
			}
			HUN = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = SVK
					autonomous_state = botde_transleithania
				}
			}
			SVK = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						HUN = { AUS_DWV_member = yes }
					}
					AUS_add_to_DWV = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						HUN = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = austrian_research }
					}
					add_to_tech_sharing_group = austrian_research
				}
				add_ideas = AUS_part_of_the_Empire
				add_ideas = AUS_transleithanian_sphere
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_conservative
				}
				increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_30 = yes
				if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_ongoing }
					set_country_flag = going_to_le_ausgleich
					add_to_array = { global.ausgleich_attendants = THIS.id }
				}
				set_variable = { AUS_subject_status = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Autonomy, Austria puppet
		name = bdeausgleich.78.d
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = AUS_release_SVK_AUS
			set_variable = { AUS.ausgleich_hungarian_revolt_slovakia_status_var = 4 }
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = SVK
				}
				transfer_state_to = SVK
			}
			AUS = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = SVK
					autonomous_state = botde_constituent
				}
			}
			SVK = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						AUS = { AUS_DWV_member = yes }
					}
					AUS_add_to_DWV = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						AUS = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = austrian_research }
					}

				}

				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {

				is_in_faction_with = var:1319.owner
				owns_state = 73
			}

				transfer_state = 73

		}

	desc = bdeausint.3.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_karl_train

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = bdeausint.3.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress > 0.8 }
				check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress = 0.8 }
			}
		}
		add_ideas = AUS_federalizing_constituent_idea
	}
	
	option = { #
		name = bdeausint.3.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress > 0.6 }
				check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress = 0.6 }
			}
			check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress < 0.8 }
		}
		add_ideas = AUS_federalizing_constituent_idea
	}
	
	option = { #
		name = bdeausint.3.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress > 0.6 }
				check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress = 0.6 }
			}
			check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress < 0.8 }
		}
		add_ideas = AUS_federalizing_constituent_idea
	}
	
	option = { #
		name = bdeausint.3.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress > 0.4 }
				check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress = 0.4 }
			}
			check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress < 0.6 }
		}
		add_ideas = AUS_federalizing_constituent_idea
	}
	
	option = { #
		name = bdeausint.3.f
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { THIS.subject_revolt_progress < 0.4 }
		}
		add_ideas = AUS_federalizing_constituent_idea

country_event = { #HIDDEN - Govt percentage
	id = bdeausint.4
	title = bdeausint.4.t
	desc = bdeausint.4.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_BAN_big_speech2

		
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Let's do this
		name = bdeausint.4.a
		AUS_raise_govt_percentage_1 = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { global.government_percentage < 1 }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausint.4
				days = 5
				random = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { global.government_percentage < 0.5 }
				check_variable = { AUS.ariosoph_power = 2 }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausdom.6
				days = 20
				random = 300
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { global.government_percentage > 0.1 }
					check_variable = { global.government_percentage = 0.1 }
				}
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = AUS_fed_speed_1
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausint.27
				days = 5
				random = 20
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { global.government_percentage > 0.4 }
					check_variable = { global.government_percentage = 0.4 }
				}
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = AUS_fed_speed_2
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausint.28
				days = 5
				random = 20
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { global.government_percentage > 0.8 }
					check_variable = { global.government_percentage = 0.8 }
				}
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = AUS_fed_speed_3
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausint.29
				days = 5
				random = 20
			}
		}
		
		
		
		
		
	}
}

country_event = { #Membership in the DWV

	desc = bdeausint.20.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_kalergi_event_pic_2

	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #YES
		name = bdeausint.20.a
		ai_chance = { base = 80 }
		AUS_add_to_DWV = yes
		ROOT_subtract_three_collapse = yes
		add_political_power = -10
		add_stability = -0.025
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = austrian_research }
				NOT = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = austrian_research }
			}
			add_to_tech_sharing_group = austrian_research
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = beausint.21
				days = 3
				random = 5
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #No
		name = bdeausint.20.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				has_variable = { ROOT.subject_revolt_progress }
				add = 80
				factor = ROOT.subject_revolt_progress
			}
			modifier = {
				AUS = { is_ai = no }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 20
		add_war_support = 0.03
		add_stability = 0.03
		ROOT_add_five_collapse = yes
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = beausint.22
				days = 3
				random = 72
			}
		}
	}
	
}

country_event = { #Formation of the Danubian Federation
	id = bdeausint.24
	title = bdeausint.24.t
	desc = bdeausint.24.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_karl_hungary_2

	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Gott erhalte Karl den Kaiser...
		name = bdeausint.24.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		add_political_power = 200
		every_core_state = {
			cancel_resistance = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = AUS_trialism_completed
			}
			AUS_federalize_trialist_effect = yes
			else = {
				AUS_federalize_effect = yes
				AUS_do_fed_name = yes
			}
		}
		#AUS_the_state_modifiers = yes
		country_event = {
			id = bdeausint.25
			days = 7
			random = 72
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					owns_state = 43
					has_government = radical_socialist
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_government = social_liberal
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_global_flag = AUS_autonomous_transleithania
							has_global_flag = AUS_autonomous_transleithania_minorities
						}
						HUN = {
							is_subject_of = AUS
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_cisleithanian_federation
			set_country_flag = AUS_federalized_cisleithania
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = AUS_ausgleich_peoples
				}
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausel.17
					days = 60
					random = 1000
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausflavor.81
				days = 90
				random_days = 90
			}
		}
	}
	
}

				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = AUS
				}
			}
		}
	}

#3 Federalizing Events
#Three Federalizing Events - each one activates a level of the "future fed speed-up"
country_event = { #The Bundeskommission Finalizes the Constitution
	id = bdeausint.27
	title = bdeausint.27.t
	desc = {
		text = bdeausint.27.d.a
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = bdeausint.27.d.b
		trigger = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = bdeausint.27.d.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_conservative
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = bdeausint.27.d.d
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_liberal
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = bdeausint.27.d.e
		trigger = {
			has_government = authoritarian_democrat
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = bdeausint.27.d.f
		trigger = {
			has_government = paternal_autocrat
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = bdeausint.27.d.g
		trigger = {
			has_government = national_populist
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = bdeausint.27.d.h
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = radical_socialist

					random = 72
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

		}
	}

country_event = { #Hidden socialist republic event
	id = bdeausint.75
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdeausint.75" }
	title = bdeausint.75.t
	desc = bdeausint.75.d
	
	hidden = yes
	
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_karl_putsch_2

	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #It's about time
		name = bdeausint.75.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_power_balance_modifier = {
						id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
						modifier = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_totalist
					}
					has_power_balance_modifier = {
						id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
						modifier = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_moderate_left
					}
					has_power_balance_modifier = {
						id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
						modifier = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_syndie
					}
					has_power_balance_modifier = {
						id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
						modifier = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_moderate_right
					}
				}
			}
			AUS_rev_progress_2 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							has_government = totalist
						}
						is_power_balance_in_range = {
							id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
							range = AUS_bop_moderate_influence_2
						}
					}
					is_power_balance_in_range = {
						id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
						range = AUS_bop_moderate_influence_3
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = THIS.anarchist_power
				value = 0.05
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							has_government = radical_socialist
						}
						is_power_balance_in_range = {
							id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
							range = AUS_bop_syndie_influence_4
						}
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							has_government = syndicalist
						}
						is_power_balance_in_range = {
							id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
							range = AUS_bop_moderate_influence_1
						}
					}
					is_power_balance_in_range = {
						id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
						range = AUS_socialist_republic_bop_neutral_influence
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = THIS.unionist_power
				value = 0.05
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							has_government = social_democrat
						}
						is_power_balance_in_range = {
							id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
							range = AUS_bop_syndie_influence_5
						}
					}
					is_power_balance_in_range = {
						id = AUS_socialist_republic_bop
						range = AUS_bop_syndie_influence_6
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = THIS.DAP_power
				value = 0.05
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_socialist_government = yes
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = AUS_DAP
						has_government = national_populist
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = AUS_DAP_revolution_stopped
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = AUS_revolution_complete
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausint.75
				days = 15
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = AWR_investigate_plot
				check_variable = { THIS.revolution_progress > 0.5 }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausint.149 #Paramilitary collusion in a plot
				days = 27
				random = 600
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { THIS.revolution_progress = 1 }
					check_variable = { THIS.revolution_progress > 1 }
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausint.150 #Revolution conclusion
			}
		}
		
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausint.146
					days = 3
					random = 200
				}
			}
			90 = {
				
			}
		}
	
		AUS_anarchist_power_3 = yes
		AUS_unionist_power_3 = yes
		AUS_DAP_power_3 = yes
		AUS_socialist_bop_random_gain = yes
		clr_country_flag = AUS_high_anarchist
		clr_country_flag = AUS_high_unionist
		clr_country_flag = AUS_high_DAP
		AUS_index_subgroup_strengths = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { THIS.anarchist_power > 0.949 }
				has_country_flag = AUS_high_anarchist
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausint.87
				days = 10
				random = 128
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { THIS.DAP_power > 0.949 }
				has_country_flag = AUS_high_DAP
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = AUS_DAP
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Walter Riehl"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausint.88
				days = 10
				random = 128
			}
		}
		
		if = {

country_event = { #DAP power max; coup or election stuff! If player took a lot of right-wing options the NatPops may come to power instead. Event will fire when DAP gets powerful, leading to Riehl normally or the NatPops if counter-revolutionary.
	id = bdeausint.85
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdeausint.85" }
	title = {
		text = bdeausint.85.t.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {  THIS.counterrev_options < 3 }
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = bdeausint.85.t.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = {  THIS.counterrev_options < 3 } }
		}
	}
	
	
	desc = {
		text = bdeausint.85.d.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {  THIS.counterrev_options < 3 }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = bdeausint.85.d.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = {  THIS.counterrev_options < 3 } }
			#using friendly DAP elements already in government, the natpops are able to get in easily and launch the coup with help from these friendly legislators
		}
	}
	
	
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_dap_event

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #A new government is formed, reinforcing the bonds of the DAP
		name = bdeausint.85.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { THIS.counterrev_options < 3 }
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
		}
		set_country_flag = AUS_DAP
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Walter Riehl"
			desc = "POLITICS_RIEHL_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/AUS/AUS_Alfred_Frauenfeld.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = volkisch_communitarianism_subtype
		}
		country_event = {
			id = bdeausint.152 #Betray the Revolution or stay with it. Party can fracture here
			days = 7
			random = 48
		}
	}
	
	option = { #NatPops seize the initiative.
		name = bdeausint.85.b
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { THIS.counterrev_options < 3 }
		}
		set_country_flag = AUS_natpops_available_revolution
		set_country_flag = AUS_DAP
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = national_populist
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		country_event = {
			id = bdeausint.86 #Choose between Frauenfeld and Glaise-Horstenau
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = { 
				ideology = totalist 
				long_name = AUS_DAP_name_long 
				name = AUS_DAP_name 
			}
			set_party_name = { 
				ideology = national_populist 
				long_name = AUS_DAP_name_long 
				name = AUS_DAP_name 
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #The DAP is fended off, but a third party comes into play.
		name = bdeausint.85.c
		country_event = {
			id = bdeausint.148
			days = 1
			random = 12
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Coup fails
		name = bdeausint.85.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Walter Riehl" ruling_only = yes } }
		}
		set_country_flag = AUS_natpops_available_revolution
	}
}

			has_country_leader = { name = "Walter Riehl" ruling_only = yes }
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Alfred Frauenfeld"
			desc = "POLITICS_FRAUENFELD_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/AUS/AUS_Alfred_Frauenfeld.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = natpop_volkisch_communitarianism_subtype
		}
		set_country_flag = AUS_alfred_frauenfeld

	option = { #Edmund Glaise-Horstenau

	option = { #A devastating blow to democracy
		name = bdeausint.94.a
		set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_VF_tag
		add_political_power = 100
		complete_national_focus = AUS_federal_state
		set_country_flag = AUS_federal_state
		set_country_flag = AUS_federal_state_dolbus
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = AUS_habsburg_law
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = AUS_monarchy_alliance
			else = {
				#Event here that forces a Heimwehr collab government, or allows Dollfuss to step down in favor of Raab/Figl.
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #And we'll do it with the Heimwehr's help!
		name = bdeausint.94.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = AUS_civil_war
				has_country_flag = AUS_habsburg_law
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_VF_tag
		add_political_power = 100
		add_war_support = 0.15
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = national_populist
			long_name = AUS_heimwehr_party_long
			name = AUS_heimwehr_party
		}
		complete_national_focus = AUS_federal_state
		set_country_flag = AUS_federal_state
		set_country_flag = AUS_heimwehr_alliance
		set_country_flag = AUS_federal_state_dolbus
	}
	
}

country_event = { #Hidden civil war (revolution) event, checks n stuff (for war's end, etc)
	id = bdeausint.95
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdeausint.95" }
	title = bdeausint.95.t
	desc = bdeausint.95.d
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_merchant_tressa

		
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = AUS_civil_war_commies_over
			has_country_flag = AUS_red_duchess
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #buh!!!
		name = bdeausint.95.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = AUS
				
				NOT = {
					country_exists = AWR
				}
				has_war = no
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = AUS_VF_coup_civilwar
				}
				country_event = bdeausint.96 #VF Civil War Ends Event
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausint.95
					days = 12
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = AWR
				
				NOT = {
					country_exists = AUS
				}
				has_war = no
			}
			country_event = bdeausint.96 #Peace event
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausint.95
					days = 12
				}
			}
		}
		
	}
}

country_event = { #Victory in the Civil War (now an umbrella. Leads to further political paths.)
	id = bdeausint.96
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdeausint.96" }
	title = {
		text = bdeausint.96.t.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = AUS_VF_coup_civilwar
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = bdeausint.96.t.a
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = AUS_absolute_crisis
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = bdeausint.96.t.a
		trigger = {
			tag = AWR
		}
	}
	desc = bdeausint.96.d
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_karl_leaving_hungary

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Austria et in orbe ultima.
		name = bdeausint.96.a
		add_political_power = 100
		add_stability = 0.25
		set_global_flag = AUS_civil_war_commies_over
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = AUS_VF_coup_civilwar
				}
				add_stability = 0.1
				add_political_power = 50
				increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
				country_event = bdeausint.157 #One Party State
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = AWR
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					AUS = {
						add_stability = 0.1
						add_political_power = 50
						increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
						set_country_flag = AWR_transfer
						every_unit_leader = {
							set_nationality = NSW
						}
						copy_government_of_ROOT = yes
						set_cosmetic_tag = AWR
						annex_country = {
							target = AWR
							transfer_troops = yes
						}
						country_event = {
							id = bdeaus.20
							days = 16
						}
						country_event = {
							id = bdeausint.71
							days = 7
						}
						country_event = {
							id = bdeausint.68
							days = 2
						}
						country_event = {
							id = bdeausint.69
							days = 30
						}
						country_event = {
							id = bdeausint.144
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_country_flag = AUS_schutzbund
							}
							country_event = {
								id = bdeausint.133 #schutzbund can retire orrrr ;)
								days = 60
								random = 250
							}
						}
					}
					every_unit_leader = {
						set_nationality = AUS
					}
					AUS = {	change_tag_from = ROOT }			
				}
			}
			#Add a clause for the Republic.
			#Add a clause for continuing military administration.
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = AUS_VF_coup_civilwar
					}
					has_global_flag = AUS_absolute_crisis
				}
				country_event = bdeausint.97 #Monarchy
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # A Monarch's Role (for the republic)
	id = bdeausint.103
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdeausint.103" }
	title = bdeausint.103.t
	desc = bdeausint.103.d
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_karl_leaving_hungary

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #The Kaiser may remain a figurehead.
		name = bdeausint.103.a
		add_political_power = -20
		set_country_flag = AUS_republic_kaiser_figurehead
	}
	
	option = { #The Kaiser will have no power or place, but may retire peacefully.
		name = bdeausint.103.b
		add_stability = -0.03
		set_country_flag = AUS_republic_kaiser_retirement
	}
	
	option = { #The Kaiser must leave!
		name = bdeausint.103.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = AUS_habsburg_law
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -10
		add_war_support = -0.03
		set_country_flag = AUS_habsburg_law
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_conservative
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
				}
			}

		has_country_flag = AUS_imminent_collapse
	}

	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Not good
		name = bdeausint.120.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		ALL_add_three_collapse = yes
		country_event = {
			id = bdeausint.121
			days = 12
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Loss of Order; Nationalist Paramilitaries Turn Out
	id = bdeausint.123
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdeausint.123" }
	title = bdeausint.123.t
	desc = bdeausint.123.d
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_suffrage
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = AUS_imminent_collapse
	}

	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #The government must push through
		name = bdeausint.123.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = minority_paramilitary_each_state
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = SLO
					NOT = {
						AUS_has_minority_paramilitary_presence = yes
					}
				}
				THIS_add_minority_paramilitary = yes
			}
			
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {

country_event = { #The Heimwehr Blocks the Inauguration (if Heimwehr has 3+ states in control and SocLib/SocDem wins)
	id = bdeausint.141
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdeausint.141" }
	title = bdeausint.141.t
	desc = bdeausint.141.d
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_karl_troops

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #The government collapses under the Heimwehr!
		name = bdeausint.141.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					AUS_habsburg_in_charge = yes
				}
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausint.143 #Kaiser intervenes
				}
				else = {
					country_event = {
						id = bdeausint.142
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #The Schutzbund intervenes!
		name = bdeausint.141.b
		trigger = {
			any_owned_state = {
				has_state_flag = AUS_schutzbund
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					AUS_habsburg_in_charge = yes
				}
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausint.143 #Kaiser intervenes
				}
				else = {
					country_event = {
						id = bdeausint.80
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.1
		}
	}
	
	option = { #The Heimwehr is beaten back.
		name = bdeausint.141.c
		add_stability = -0.06
		add_political_power = -50
	}
	
}

country_event = { #Counter-Revolutionary Activities (This event should fire with the random socialist republic ticker event.)
	id = bdeausint.146
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdeausint.146" }
	title = bdeausint.146.t
	desc = bdeausint.146.d
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_karl_troops

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #A real thorn in the side
		name = bdeausint.146.a
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						arms_factory > 0
						OR = {
							has_state_flag = AUS_sturmscharen
							has_state_flag = AUS_heimwehr
							has_state_flag = AUS_frontfighters
							has_state_flag = AUS_ordo_novi_templi
						}
					}
					damage_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						damage = 4
					}
				}
			}
			
			50 = {
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						industrial_complex > 0
						OR = {
							has_state_flag = AUS_sturmscharen
							has_state_flag = AUS_heimwehr
							has_state_flag = AUS_frontfighters
							has_state_flag = AUS_ordo_novi_templi
						}
					}
					damage_building = {
						type = industrial_complex
						damage = 2
					}
				}
			}
		}

	}
}

			id = bdeausint.80
		}

		name = bdeausint.153.b

			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var =  THIS.counterrev_options
			value = 1
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Heimwehr Militias Offer to Fight (Civil War)
	id = bdeausint.155
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdeausint.155" }
	title = bdeausint.155.t
	desc = bdeausint.155.d
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_karl_troops

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #They can fight alongside us
		name = bdeausint.155.a
		add_political_power = -40
		add_stability = 0.05
		division_template = {
			name = "Heimwehrmiliz"
			is_locked = yes
			regiments = {
				militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }
			}
			support = {
				military_police = { x = 0 y = 0 }
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			create_unit = { 
				division = "name = \"Heimwehrmiliz\" division_template = \"Heimwehrmiliz\" start_experience_factor = 0.75" 
				owner = AUS
			}
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			create_unit = { 
				division = "name = \"Heimwehrmiliz\" division_template = \"Heimwehrmiliz\" start_experience_factor = 0.75" 
				owner = AUS
			}
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			create_unit = { 
				division = "name = \"Heimwehrmiliz\" division_template = \"Heimwehrmiliz\" start_experience_factor = 0.75" 
				owner = AUS
			}
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			create_unit = { 
				division = "name = \"Heimwehrmiliz\" division_template = \"Heimwehrmiliz\" start_experience_factor = 0.75" 
				owner = AUS
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
				var = AUS.heimwehr_count
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #We do not need them
		name = bdeausint.155.b
		add_political_power = 35
	}
	
}

country_event = { #Assassination Attempt on Engelbert Dollfuss
	id = bdeausint.158
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdeausint.158" }
	title = bdeausint.158.t
	desc = bdeausint.158.d
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_cult

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #The assassination succeeds!
		name = bdeausint.158.a
		kill_country_leader = yes
		set_country_flag = AUS_dollfuss_assassinated
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_political_power = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = AUS.heimwehr_count
						value = 1
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					has_country_flag = AUS_heimwehr_alliance
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Emil Fey"
				desc = "POLITICS_FEY_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/AUS/AUS_Emil_Fey.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = austropopulism_subtype
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bdeausint.159 #The Heimwehr State
			}
			else = {
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Kurt Schuschnigg"
					desc = "POLITICS_SCHUSCHNIGG_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/AUS/AUS_Kurt_Schuschnigg.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = austropopulism_subtype
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #The assassination fails!
		name = bdeausint.158.b
		add_war_support = 0.15
		add_political_power = -50
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_3 = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #A Heimwehr Government Rises

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdeausint.159" }

	}
}

country_event = { #The E.M.F. Project Begins
	id = bdeausflavor.9
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdeausflavor.9" }
	title = bdeausflavor.9.t
	desc = bdeausflavor.9.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_atomic_fission

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Operation A.E.I.O.U. is a go.
		name = bdeausflavor.9.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_dlc = "Gotterdammerung"
				}
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				category = nuclear
				bonus = 1
				uses = 1
				ahead_reduction = 1.5
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausflavor.11
					days = 1250
					random = 10000
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_tech_bonus = {
				category = nuclear
				bonus = 0.85
				uses = 1
				ahead_reduction = 2
			}
			sp:sp_nuclear_bomb = {
				add_project_progress_ratio = 0.15
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 775
				}
				775 = {
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = AUS_innsbruck_project }
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								nuclear_facility > 0
							}
							remove_building = {
								type = nuclear_facility
								level = 1
							}
						}
						AUS_remove_paramilitaries = yes
						increase_state_category = yes
						add_building_construction = {
							type = supply_node
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
							province = 6691
						}
					}
					add_building_construction = {
						type = nuclear_facility
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
						province = 6691
					}
					build_railway = {
						level = 1
						path = { 13575 9679 9650 6691 }
						start_province = 13575
						target_province = 6691
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Dropping of the "Frederick III" Atomic Bomb
	id = bdeausflavor.11	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdeausflavor.11" }
	title = bdeausflavor.11.t
	desc = bdeausflavor.11.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_AUS_bomb_tower

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			launch_nuke = {
				province = 6687
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Now I am become Death, destroyer of worlds.
		name = bdeausflavor.11.a
		add_nuclear_bombs = 1
		every_state = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = AUS_innsbruck_project } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = AUS_innsbruck_project }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_owned_state = {
						has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = fallout_atomic }
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = fallout_atomic } }
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = fallout_atomic }
					add_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = fallout_atomic
						days = 14
					}
				}
			}
			GER = {
				country_event = {
					id = bdeausflavor.12
					days = 1
					random_days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = bdeausflavor.12.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #What could it mean?
		name = bdeausflavor.12.a
		add_stability = -0.01
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
